  - 🔍 High contrast: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-contrast: more`

## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 50 page(s) - 100 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)
**Issue**: The element does not have a unique ID

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<div id="lgd-header__nav--primary" class="lgd-header__nav lgd-header__nav--primary">...</div>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/div[@id="lgd-header__nav--primary"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/div[@id="lgd-header__nav--primary"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://www.kingston.gov.uk/
- https://www.kingston.gov.uk/news/2025/quicker-and-easier-every-step-way-kingston-council-launches-new-website
- https://www.kingston.gov.uk/your-council/elections-and-voting/upcoming-elections/timetable
- https://www.kingston.gov.uk/planning-and-building-control/planning-policy/authority-monitoring-report
- https://www.kingston.gov.uk/news/2023/celebrating-kingstons-cinematic-heritage-pioneering-photographer-eadweard-muybridge-archive-open-public
- *...and 45 more page(s)*

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)
**Issue**: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://www.kingston.gov.uk/

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_close" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-label="Close">×</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_close"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_accept" tabindex="0" role="button" data-cs-i18n-text="{"en":"Accept all"}">         Accept all      </div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_accept"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_reject" tabindex="0" role="button" data-cs-i18n-text="{"en":"Decline all"}">         Decline all      </div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_reject"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_manage_wrap" tabindex="0" role="button">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_manage_wrap"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button type="submit" class="btn btn--solid notranslate" aria-label="Submit translation request">         Go       </button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="btn btn--solid notranslate"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)
**WCAG**: [SC 4.1.2](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/name-role-value) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)
**WCAG**: [SC 3.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/language-of-page) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div id="lgd-header__nav--primary" class="lgd-header__nav lgd-header__nav--primary">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="lgd-header__nav--primary"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<nav aria-labelledby="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk" class="block block-menu navigation navigation--main">...</nav>`
- XPath: `/nav[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<h2 class="visually-hidden" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu">Main navigation</h2>`
- XPath: `/h2[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div class="views-exposed-form bef-exposed-form block block-views block-views-exposed-filter-blocksearch-block-2" data-drupal-selector="views-exposed-form-search-block-2" id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div data-drupal-selector="edit-actions--2" class="form-actions js-form-wrapper form-wrapper" id="edit-actions--2--XSnamGTwmQo">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="edit-actions--2--XSnamGTwmQo"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R56: Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `contentinfo` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R61: Documents start with a level 1 heading](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61)
**WCAG**: Best Practice

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document does not start with a level 1 heading

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 6.42:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>Find local support groups, useful services, and ge...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>Construction of the new Kingston Leisure Centre is...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R80: ASCII art has a text alternative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r80)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>Construction of the new Kingston Leisure Centre is...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R83: Text can be resized to 200% without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r83)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.4](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/resize-text) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is clipped

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.4.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/bypass-blocks) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

### https://www.kingston.gov.uk/your-council/elections-and-voting/upcoming-elections/timetable

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://kingston.us2.list-manage.com/subscribe?u=4f9693900f570d3a4ca3b6e39&id=d51fd21b38" class="ext" data-extlink="" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ext"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<select class="gt_selector notranslate" aria-label="Select Language">...</select>`
- XPath: `/select[@class="gt_selector notranslate"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/your-council/contact-us" target="_self" data-drupal-link-system-path="node/1099">Contact us</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_close" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-label="Close">×</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_close"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_accept" tabindex="0" role="button" data-cs-i18n-text="{"en":"Accept all"}">         Accept all      </div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_accept"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID

- HTML: `<button class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary" data-target="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-controls="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Services: jump to services" data-once="header-toggle">...</button>`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name

- XPath: `/a[@class="document-link button button-tertiary"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button type="submit" class="btn btn--solid notranslate" aria-label="Submit translation request">         Go       </button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="btn btn--solid notranslate"]`

**Failure 1:**

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_close" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-label="Close">×</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_close"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_accept" tabindex="0" role="button" data-cs-i18n-text="{"en":"Accept all"}">         Accept all      </div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_accept"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_reject" tabindex="0" role="button" data-cs-i18n-text="{"en":"Decline all"}">         Decline all      </div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_reject"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_manage_wrap" tabindex="0" role="button">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_manage_wrap"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary" data-target="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-controls="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Services: jump to services" data-once="header-toggle">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button type="submit" class="btn btn--solid notranslate" aria-label="Submit translation request">         Go       </button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="btn btn--solid notranslate"]`

**Failure 1:**

### https://www.kingston.gov.uk/housing/arriving-in-uk/support-for-ukrainians/homes-for-ukraine-future-accommodation-options/continue-with-current-host

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#bbd-translation-form" class="button-link">Translate</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="button-link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/housing/arriving-in-uk/support-for-ukrainians/homes-for-ukraine-future-accommodation-options" hreflang="en-gb">Future housing options</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#/" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#collapseFeedback" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="collapseFeedback" class="reveal">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="reveal"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://kingston.us2.list-manage.com/subscribe?u=4f9693900f570d3a4ca3b6e39&id=d51fd21b38" class="ext" data-extlink="" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ext"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<select class="gt_selector notranslate" aria-label="Select Language">...</select>`
- XPath: `/select[@class="gt_selector notranslate"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary" data-target="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-controls="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Services: jump to services" data-once="header-toggle">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button type="submit" class="btn btn--solid notranslate" aria-label="Submit translation request">         Go       </button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="btn btn--solid notranslate"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)
**WCAG**: [SC 4.1.2](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/name-role-value) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)
**WCAG**: [SC 3.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/language-of-page) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div id="lgd-header__nav--primary" class="lgd-header__nav lgd-header__nav--primary">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="lgd-header__nav--primary"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<nav aria-labelledby="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk" class="block block-menu navigation navigation--main">...</nav>`
- XPath: `/nav[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<h2 class="visually-hidden" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu">Main navigation</h2>`
- XPath: `/h2[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div class="views-exposed-form bef-exposed-form block block-views block-views-exposed-filter-blocksearch-block-2" data-drupal-selector="views-exposed-form-search-block-2" id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div data-drupal-selector="edit-actions" class="form-actions js-form-wrapper form-wrapper" id="edit-actions--_MXtBGWkh54">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="edit-actions--_MXtBGWkh54"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R61: Documents start with a level 1 heading](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61)
**WCAG**: Best Practice

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document does not start with a level 1 heading

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.75:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="lgd-page-title-block__subheader">Explore longer-term housing options for your guest...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="lgd-page-title-block__subheader"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="lgd-page-title-block__subheader">Explore longer-term housing options for your guest...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="lgd-page-title-block__subheader"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>Following a discussion with your host, you may be ...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R78: Headings of same level have text content between them](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r78)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/info-and-relationships) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: There is no content between this heading and the next
- HTML: `<h2 class="lgd-guides__title">         Option 1: Continue with current host, if ...</h2>`
- XPath: `/h2[@class="lgd-guides__title"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R80: ASCII art has a text alternative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r80)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="lgd-page-title-block__subheader">Explore longer-term housing options for your guest...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="lgd-page-title-block__subheader"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>Following a discussion with your host, you may be ...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.4.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/bypass-blocks) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

### https://www.kingston.gov.uk/planning-and-building-control/planning-applications/homeowner/fast-track-your-planning-application/service-requirements

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#/" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#collapseFeedback" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="collapseFeedback" class="reveal">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="reveal"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://kingston.us2.list-manage.com/subscribe?u=4f9693900f570d3a4ca3b6e39&id=d51fd21b38" class="ext" data-extlink="" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="ext"]`

**Failure 3:**

- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_close" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-label="Close">×</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_close"]`

**Failure 2:**

- HTML: `<a href="/sites/default/files/2025-04/RBK_Views_Study_Report_Appendix_H_VHIV_Pro_Formas.pdf" class="document-link button button-tertiary" aria-label="RBK_Views_Study_Report_Appendix_H_VHIV_Pro_Formas" target="_blank">         Download       </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="document-link button button-tertiary"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button type="submit" class="btn btn--solid notranslate" aria-label="Submit translation request">         Go       </button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="btn btn--solid notranslate"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)
**WCAG**: [SC 4.1.2](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/name-role-value) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)
**WCAG**: [SC 3.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/language-of-page) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div id="lgd-header__nav--primary" class="lgd-header__nav lgd-header__nav--primary">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="lgd-header__nav--primary"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<nav aria-labelledby="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk" class="block block-menu navigation navigation--main">...</nav>`
- XPath: `/nav[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<h2 class="visually-hidden" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu">Main navigation</h2>`
- XPath: `/h2[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div class="views-exposed-form bef-exposed-form block block-views block-views-exposed-filter-blocksearch-block-2" data-drupal-selector="views-exposed-form-search-block-2" id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div data-drupal-selector="edit-actions" class="form-actions js-form-wrapper form-wrapper" id="edit-actions--ucjC2mlohYM">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="edit-actions--ucjC2mlohYM"]`

- HTML: `<div data-drupal-selector="edit-actions" class="form-actions js-form-wrapper form-wrapper" id="edit-actions--uhZalEj5Ri4">...</div>`

#### Rule: [SIA-R80: ASCII art has a text alternative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r80)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="lgd-page-title-block__subheader">Get full detail of our standards and policies, inc...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="lgd-page-title-block__subheader"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>‘Safeguarding’ is a term which covers the full ran...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is clipped

**Failure 1:**

### https://www.kingston.gov.uk/care-support-for-adults/paying-for-social-care/paying-care-home-or-community

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_close" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-label="Close">×</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_close"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_accept" tabindex="0" role="button" data-cs-i18n-text="{"en":"Accept all"}">         Accept all      </div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_accept"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_reject" tabindex="0" role="button" data-cs-i18n-text="{"en":"Decline all"}">         Decline all      </div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_reject"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_manage_wrap" tabindex="0" role="button">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_manage_wrap"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary" data-target="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-controls="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Services: jump to services" data-once="header-toggle">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button type="submit" class="btn btn--solid notranslate" aria-label="Submit translation request">         Go       </button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="btn btn--solid notranslate"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)
**WCAG**: [SC 4.1.2](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/name-role-value) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)
**WCAG**: [SC 3.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/language-of-page) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div id="lgd-header__nav--primary" class="lgd-header__nav lgd-header__nav--primary">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="lgd-header__nav--primary"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<nav aria-labelledby="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk" class="block block-menu navigation navigation--main">...</nav>`
- XPath: `/nav[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<h2 class="visually-hidden" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu">Main navigation</h2>`
- XPath: `/h2[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div class="views-exposed-form bef-exposed-form block block-views block-views-exposed-filter-blocksearch-block-2" data-drupal-selector="views-exposed-form-search-block-2" id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div data-drupal-selector="edit-actions" class="form-actions js-form-wrapper form-wrapper" id="edit-actions--nTMQQnI2kPo">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="edit-actions--nTMQQnI2kPo"]`

- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_accept"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_reject" tabindex="0" role="button" data-cs-i18n-text="{"en":"Decline all"}">         Decline all      </div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_reject"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_manage_wrap" tabindex="0" role="button">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_manage_wrap"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary" data-target="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-controls="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Services: jump to services" data-once="header-toggle">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button type="submit" class="btn btn--solid notranslate" aria-label="Submit translation request">         Go       </button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="btn btn--solid notranslate"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)
**WCAG**: [SC 4.1.2](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/name-role-value) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

- HTML: `<nav aria-labelledby="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk" class="block block-menu navigation navigation--main">...</nav>`
- XPath: `/nav[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<h2 class="visually-hidden" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu">Main navigation</h2>`
- XPath: `/h2[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div class="views-exposed-form bef-exposed-form block block-views block-views-exposed-filter-blocksearch-block-2" data-drupal-selector="views-exposed-form-search-block-2" id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div data-drupal-selector="edit-actions" class="form-actions js-form-wrapper form-wrapper" id="edit-actions--txkRVmWY8zY">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="edit-actions--txkRVmWY8zY"]`

- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_accept"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_reject" tabindex="0" role="button" data-cs-i18n-text="{"en":"Decline all"}">         Decline all      </div>`

**Failure 1:**

- HTML: `<button class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary" data-target="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-controls="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Services: jump to services" data-once="header-toggle">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button type="submit" class="btn btn--solid notranslate" aria-label="Submit translation request">         Go       </button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="btn btn--solid notranslate"]`

- Message: Target has insufficient size

**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**

- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_close" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-label="Close">×</div>`

- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_accept" tabindex="0" role="button" data-cs-i18n-text="{"en":"Accept all"}">         Accept all      </div>`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_reject" tabindex="0" role="button" data-cs-i18n-text="{"en":"Decline all"}">         Decline all      </div>`

**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary" data-target="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-controls="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Services: jump to services" data-once="header-toggle">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button type="submit" class="btn btn--solid notranslate" aria-label="Submit translation request">         Go       </button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="btn btn--solid notranslate"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<h2 class="visually-hidden" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu">Main navigation</h2>`
- XPath: `/h2[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div class="views-exposed-form bef-exposed-form block block-views block-views-exposed-filter-blocksearch-block-2" data-drupal-selector="views-exposed-form-search-block-2" id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div data-drupal-selector="edit-actions" class="form-actions js-form-wrapper form-wrapper" id="edit-actions--b6XolAUuQFI">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="edit-actions--b6XolAUuQFI"]`

- XPath: `/p[@class="lgd-page-title-block__subheader"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p dir="ltr">You’ll need to tell us when:</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 1:**

- HTML: `<button class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary" data-target="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-controls="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Services: jump to services" data-once="header-toggle">...</button>`

- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_accept" tabindex="0" role="button" data-cs-i18n-text="{"en":"Accept all"}">         Accept all      </div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_accept"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_reject" tabindex="0" role="button" data-cs-i18n-text="{"en":"Decline all"}">         Decline all      </div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_reject"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_manage_wrap" tabindex="0" role="button">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_manage_wrap"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary" data-target="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-controls="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Services: jump to services" data-once="header-toggle">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button type="submit" class="btn btn--solid notranslate" aria-label="Submit translation request">         Go       </button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="btn btn--solid notranslate"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)
**WCAG**: [SC 4.1.2](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/name-role-value) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)
**WCAG**: [SC 3.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/language-of-page) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**

- HTML: `<nav aria-labelledby="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk" class="block block-menu navigation navigation--main">...</nav>`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID

- XPath: `/h2[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div class="views-exposed-form bef-exposed-form block block-views block-views-exposed-filter-blocksearch-block-2" data-drupal-selector="views-exposed-form-search-block-2" id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div data-drupal-selector="edit-actions" class="form-actions js-form-wrapper form-wrapper" id="edit-actions--4eym0iNS2Co">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="edit-actions--4eym0iNS2Co"]`

- HTML: `<nav aria-labelledby="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk" class="block block-menu navigation navigation--main">...</nav>`
- XPath: `/nav[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<h2 class="visually-hidden" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu">Main navigation</h2>`
- XPath: `/h2[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div class="views-exposed-form bef-exposed-form block block-views block-views-exposed-filter-blocksearch-block-2" data-drupal-selector="views-exposed-form-search-block-2" id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div data-drupal-selector="edit-actions" class="form-actions js-form-wrapper form-wrapper" id="edit-actions--AYl-1t0rW-k">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="edit-actions--AYl-1t0rW-k"]`

- HTML: `<p class="lgd-page-title-block__subheader">Find out what personal information we collect and ...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="lgd-page-title-block__subheader"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>This privacy notice sets out how the Kingston and ...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R80: ASCII art has a text alternative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r80)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="lgd-page-title-block__subheader">Find out what personal information we collect and ...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="lgd-page-title-block__subheader"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>This privacy notice sets out how the Kingston and ...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.4.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/bypass-blocks) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

### https://www.kingston.gov.uk/events/move-well-live-well-new-malden-spring-event

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_close" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-label="Close">×</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_close"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_accept" tabindex="0" role="button" data-cs-i18n-text="{"en":"Accept all"}">         Accept all      </div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_accept"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_reject" tabindex="0" role="button" data-cs-i18n-text="{"en":"Decline all"}">         Decline all      </div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_reject"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<div id="cookiescript_manage_wrap" tabindex="0" role="button">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="cookiescript_manage_wrap"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary" data-target="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-controls="lgd-header__nav--secondary" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Services: jump to services" data-once="header-toggle">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="lgd-header__toggle lgd-header__toggle--secondary"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<button type="submit" class="btn btn--solid notranslate" aria-label="Submit translation request">         Go       </button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="btn btn--solid notranslate"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)
**WCAG**: [SC 4.1.2](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/name-role-value) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)
**WCAG**: [SC 3.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/language-of-page) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div id="lgd-header__nav--primary" class="lgd-header__nav lgd-header__nav--primary">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="lgd-header__nav--primary"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<nav aria-labelledby="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk" class="block block-menu navigation navigation--main">...</nav>`
- XPath: `/nav[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<h2 class="visually-hidden" id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu">Main navigation</h2>`
- XPath: `/h2[@id="block-bbd-localgov-localgov-mainnavigation-scarfolk-menu"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div class="views-exposed-form bef-exposed-form block block-views block-views-exposed-filter-blocksearch-block-2" data-drupal-selector="views-exposed-form-search-block-2" id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="block-bbd-localgov-exposedformsearchblock-2"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div data-drupal-selector="edit-actions" class="form-actions js-form-wrapper form-wrapper" id="edit-actions--U8SK1cUtJqI">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="edit-actions--U8SK1cUtJqI"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R56: Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/identify-purpose) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `contentinfo` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R61: Documents start with a level 1 heading](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61)
**WCAG**: Best Practice

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document does not start with a level 1 heading

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 6.42:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="lgd-page-title-block__subheader">Move Well, Live Well New Malden is a free event, w...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="lgd-page-title-block__subheader"]`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: autocomplete attribute must be used correctly
- HTML: `<input class="mapControlManager__input k-input" style="width: 100%;" data-role="autocomplete" placeholder="Address, Post code or Name" type="text" autocomplete="!" role="textbox" aria-haspopup="true" aria-disabled="false" aria-readonly="false" aria-autocomplete="list" aria-owns="">`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img class="legendTab__preview" src="data:image/png;base6...">`
- XPath: `#map`

- XPath: `footer`
